It extends URLClassLoader and maintains a reference to the plugin location.\\n   - DelegatingClassLoader: Acts as a parent classloader that delegates to multiple PluginClassLoaders, implementing child-first delegation to prioritize isolated plugins.\\n   - ClassLoaderFactory: Factory for creating DelegatingClassLoader and PluginClassLoader instances, supporting mocking in tests.\\n   - LoaderSwap: Try-with-resources helper for temporarily switching thread context classloaders during plugin initialization and configuration.\\n\\n2. **Plugin Discovery and Scanning Layer**:\\n   - PluginScanner (abstract): Base class for plugin discovery implementations with common functionality for merging results from multiple sources.\\n   - ReflectionScanner: Uses ClassGraph library for reflection-based scanning of classpath and plugin jars to discover implementations of plugin interfaces (SinkConnector, SourceConnector, Converter, HeaderConverter, Transformation, Predicate, ConfigProvider, ConnectRestExtension, ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy).\\n   - ServiceLoaderScanner: Uses Java's ServiceLoader mechanism for discovering plugins with proper META-INF/services manifests (more performant but requires manifest files).\\n   - PluginSource: Record class defining plugin sources with type (CLASSPATH, MULTI_JAR, SINGLE_JAR, CLASS_HIERARCHY), loader, and URLs.\\n   - PluginScanResult: Container for plugin discovery results organized by type (sinkConnectors, sourceConnectors, converters, headerConverters, transformations, predicates, configProviders, restExtensions, connectorClientConfigPolicies).\\n\\n3. **Plugin Management Layer**:\\n   - Plugins: Main orchestrator managing plugin discovery, instantiation, and configuration. It coordinates between ReflectionScanner/ServiceLoaderScanner and DelegatingClassLoader.\\n   - PluginDesc<T>: Descriptor class for discovered plugins containing class reference, name, version, type, and loader. Implements Comparable for version-aware sorting.\\n   - PluginType: Enum defining plugin categories (SOURCE, SINK, CONVERTER, HEADER_CONVERTER, TRANSFORMATION, PREDICATE, CONFIGPROVIDER, REST_EXTENSION, CONNECTOR_CLIENT_CONFIG_OVERRIDE_POLICY), each mapped to its base interface class.\\n   - PluginDiscoveryMode: Enum controlling discovery strategy (ONLY_SCAN for reflection only, HYBRID_WARN/HYBRID_FAIL for combined reflection and ServiceLoader with compatibility checking).\\n   - PluginUtils: Utility class providing helper methods for plugin manipulation, isolation detection, filtering, and alias computation.\\n\\n4. **Plugin Interfaces** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/):\\n   - Connector: Base interface for all connectors with lifecycle methods (start, stop, taskClass, taskConfigs, config).\\n   - SinkConnector/SourceConnector: Specialized connector interfaces for data sink and source operations.\\n   - Converter: Interface for translating between Kafka Connect's runtime data format and byte arrays, discoverable via ServiceLoader.\\n   - HeaderConverter: Similar to Converter but specifically for header values, with implementation examples like SimpleHeaderConverter.\\n   - Transformation<R>: Generic interface for record transformations (extends Configurable, Closeable), supporting service loading via META-INF/services.\\n   - Predicate<R>: Interface for conditional transformation application, allowing selective application of transformations.\\n   - ConnectRestExtension: Interface for REST API extensions, discovered via ServiceLoader mechanism.\\n   - ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy: Interface for enforcing Kafka client configuration policies.\\n\\n5. **Dependency Injection and Configuration**:\\n   - All plugin interfaces extend org.apache.kafka.common.Configurable for configuration management with ConfigDef specifications.\\n   - Plugin wrapper class (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/internals/Plugin.java): Generic wrapper implementing Supplier<T> for plugin instances with metrics integration.\\n   - ConnectMetrics: Metrics framework for tracking plugin usage (PluginMetrics class wraps plugin instances with automatic metric registration for converters, transformations, predicates).\\n   - WorkerConfig: Centralized configuration with PLUGIN_PATH_CONFIG for specifying isolation directories and PLUGIN_DISCOVERY_CONFIG for choosing discovery strategy.\\n   - TaskPluginsMetadata and TransformationStage: Runtime structures managing plugin instances for task execution, including predicate chaining and conditional transformation.\\n\\nThe system supports multi-versioning through VersionRange specifications, allowing different plugin versions to coexist. Isolation is achieved through separate PluginClassLoaders with child-first delegation, preventing version conflicts between plugins and the framework. Configuration is injected via standard Configurable interface, and plugins are discovered either reflectively (slower but no manifest requirement) or via ServiceLoader (faster but requires manifests). The dependency injection is implicit through interface contracts and explicit through the ConfigDef specification mechanism, enabling flexible plugin composition and configuration validation.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":506,"cache_read_input_tokens":110510,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":506},"output_tokens":4,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"0374e9d8-7a10-4659-9195-53470dc5a89b","uuid":"8ebb6347-e9d0-4856-8da2-91eff67f7436"}
